        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</section>
</aside>

</p><p><b>Silvers Rayleigh</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-romanized_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-romanized-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> also known as the <b>"Dark King"</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-c501_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c501-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> is an extremely powerful and famous retired <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a> who formerly served as the <a href="/wiki/First_Mate" title="First Mate">first mate</a> of the legendary <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-retell_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-retell-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> being known as the "Right Hand of the Pirate King".<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He is one of the major figures, along with <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a> from the times when <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, the "Pirate King", was still alive.
</p><p>After the disbandment of the Roger Pirates and the execution of Gol D. Roger, Rayleigh became a <a href="/wiki/Coating" title="Coating">coating mechanic</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>. Also, at some point after this, he became the husband of <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> and befriended <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-marriage_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marriage-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh is an ally of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc" title="Sabaody Archipelago Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</a> and served as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s mentor in the use of <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> during the two-year timeskip.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Rayleigh is an elderly man of relatively tall height with a very muscular build and tan skin. Two of his most distinguishing traits are his round glasses and facial hair, which is arranged embattled across his lower jaw. He also has a scar over his right eye, which he has had for many years.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh chooses to dress quite simply, usually just in a nearly plain t-shirt, shorts, and sandals. When out in public, he also seems to enjoy the cover of a large silver hooded cloak, though the hood is often down. Underneath these clothes, the old man's body is surprisingly built and very well-toned, a testament to his incredible strength.
</p><p>When Rayleigh was younger, he had clean cut strawberry blond hair (black when first seen in the anime) and had a moderate amount of facial hair. Over the years, as his hair whitened, he grew it out. He also grew a beard from his initial striped facial hair. During Roger's last year alive, Rayleigh was noticeably taller, reaching almost the same height as his former captain. Regardless of his age, Rayleigh is a muscular man with a broad chest and well-built body.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During Rayleigh's first appearance in Buggy's flashback, he wore a t-shirt with an ornately decorated collar, a motif that appeared even in the long coat he wore during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Edd_War" title="Battle of Edd War">Battle of Edd War</a>. He wore an orange shirt, light-brown spotted bermudas, and simple sandals. He also has a silver-colored coat hanging from his shoulders.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the two-year timeskip, Rayleigh now wears a black T-shirt as well as his silver hooded cloak.
</p><p>Later after the <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a> and his arrival on <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a>, Rayleigh wore a yellow ochre top with sleeves and light-green pants with dark green zig-zag like diamond patterns.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Silvers_Rayleigh_Manga_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest?cb=20230327224327" class="image"><img alt="Silvers Rayleigh Manga Color Scheme" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="69" data-image-name="Silvers Rayleigh Manga Color Scheme.png" data-image-key="Silvers_Rayleigh_Manga_Color_Scheme.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Silvers_Rayleigh_Manga_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20230327224327" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Rayleigh's color scheme in the manga.

<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8e/Silvers_Rayleigh_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20191107232642" class="image"><img alt="Silvers Rayleigh Anime Concept Art" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="60" height="105" data-image-name="Silvers Rayleigh Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Silvers_Rayleigh_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8e/Silvers_Rayleigh_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/60?cb=20191107232642" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Silvers Rayleigh's concept art from the anime.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Rayleigh is light-hearted, casual, and fun loving, much like his captain <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Roger</a> was. In the past, he was shown to have been impatient with the antics of the younger crew members and took the position of crew disciplinarian very seriously. However, he has changed his personality in his older years, becoming much more relaxed even when training <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>.
</p><p>Though he often has a serious air, Rayleigh enjoys going with the flow and appearing in unexpected places and in unexpected ways, especially given his status and age. He often comments on his age and how his body "does not work the way it used to", much like <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a>.
</p><p>Rayleigh is not often headstrong, looking before he leaps and taking time to plan ahead before taking action, although he does not hesitate to act if needs be. Even when entering into an unfortunate or unplanned situation such as engaging a Marine admiral in combat or having his ship sink in the Sea King infested waters of the Grand Line, Rayleigh remains completely calm, pushing forward through adversity with no hesitation. However, Rayleigh has something of a fatherly side to him. This is shown when it comes to Luffy and Hancock, and when pushed, Rayleigh is capable of anger when provoked. When Blackbeard invaded Amazon Lily and tried to kill Hancock, Rayleigh stared furiously towards him, even referring him as a brat whom he did not like.
</p><p>He is typically open and talkative, and like <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, seems to enjoy talking about the past and its great times, as well as the good old days of their near-bygone era. In spite of this, he appeared reluctant to get into the darker topic of the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>. He was willing to divulge the whole truth to Nico Robin if she wished, but she declined his offer. Like Whitebeard, he is also aware of his own limitations that he is far past his prime. In spite of his legendary status, Rayleigh admitted he would be no match for Blackbeard in a straight up fight at his age and was gambling on his reputation to scare him off.
</p><p>As stated by <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakky</a>, he loves alcohol and women, which he proved when he is first introduced saving <a href="/wiki/Camie" title="Camie">Camie</a> from being mistreated by <a href="/wiki/Disco" title="Disco">Disco</a> while holding a hip flask. He prefers to be called "Ray-san". Despite once being enemies with the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, Rayleigh seems to have great respect for their captain, like Roger, and shed a tear for Whitebeard's passing.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Roger_Pirates">Roger Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Rayleigh's relationship with most of the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> is unknown. However, he had a close relationship with his captain <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>. He later became the <a href="/wiki/First_Mate" title="First Mate">first mate</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Oro_Jackson" title="Oro Jackson">Oro Jackson</a>, the ship of the man who would conquer the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> and be crowned by the world as the <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gol_D._Roger">Gol D. Roger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh had an incredibly close relationship with Roger knowing each other for many decades, to the point where he was called 'partner' by the Pirate King. After the man gave himself to the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, Rayleigh was unable to bring himself to directly witness the execution of his closest friend. He toasted a drink to the man with both tears and laughter as the blades passed and downed a glass as his first act in <a href="/wiki/Pirate#The_Golden_Age_of_Piracy" title="Pirate">the Great Age of Piracy</a>, the Age of Dreams.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Buggy_and_Shanks">Buggy and Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>During their times as pirate apprentices on the ship, their repeated bickering with each other often led to them being punished by Rayleigh.
</p><p>Despite that, <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> still has much respect for the former first mate of the crew. Rayleigh was aware that Buggy was a pirate in the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>, which means he kept tabs on him. Twelve years ago, after <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> saved Luffy from being eaten by the <a href="/wiki/Lord_of_the_Coast" title="Lord of the Coast">Lord of the Coast</a>, Shanks reunited with Rayleigh at Sabaody Archipelago and told him about a <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">boy</a> he met in East Blue, and after their conversation, Rayleigh became curious to meet Luffy.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Crocus">Crocus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>He seems to appreciate <a href="/wiki/Crocus" title="Crocus">Crocus</a> for maintaining the Pirate King's health during their voyage in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>. Despite the doctor's brief time with them, he considers him a valued crewmate and expressed a desire to see him again.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Oden">Kouzuki Oden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Like the rest of the crew, he held <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Oden</a> in high regard. Rayleigh wanted to help him make <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> open to the rest of the world though Oden declined the offer.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> is Rayleigh’s business partner and wife.<sup id="cite_ref-marriage_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marriage-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> When he had gone missing for the previous six months before her introduction, she was not worried because she knew what Rayleigh is capable of. Upon meeting Luffy, she informed him of the other major pirates (the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Eleven Supernovas</a>) that had arrived on the island around the same time as him. She then told them that they might find Rayleigh at <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Park" title="Sabaody Park">Sabaody Park</a>. After the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> returned from the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a>, where they found Rayleigh, he and the entire Straw Hat crew gathered at Shakky's bar. Rayleigh trusts her implicitly and he knows her qualities. With her deductions, Rayleigh managed to find Luffy after the war.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends">Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hatchan">Hatchan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a> is friends with Silvers Rayleigh, after saving the pirate from a shipwreck as a child. Since then, the two were on good terms, but Rayleigh disapproved of Hatchan joining <a href="/wiki/Fisher_Tiger" title="Fisher Tiger">Fisher Tiger</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sun_Pirates" title="Sun Pirates">Sun Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After meeting them during the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auction_House" class="mw-redirect" title="Human Auction House">Human Auctioning House</a> incident, Rayleigh assisted the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> on several occasions. He coated the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> for free and he also defended the crew from <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>. After the Straw Hats got back together two years after the Summit War of Marineford, he taught <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> the technicalities of sailing a coated ship. When the Marines pursued the crew, Rayleigh helped the Straw Hats escape.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png/revision/latest?cb=20241117020653" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh and Luffy Bonding" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh and Luffy Bonding.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020653" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png/revision/latest?cb=20241117020653" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh and Luffy Bonding" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020653" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh and Luffy Bonding.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020653" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_and_Luffy_Bonding.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh and Luffy bonding during the timeskip.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ever since Rayleigh had heard about <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> from Shanks, he had wanted to meet him face to face. When Luffy found him on the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, he was excited about hearing stories about Gol D. Roger. The more they talked, the more amused Rayleigh felt as he compared Luffy's demeanor to his old captain just as Shanks had. He, like Shakky, has great expectations for him after Luffy stated his belief that the <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a> has the most freedom on the sea. After the war at Marineford, he swam across the <a href="/wiki/Calm_Belt" title="Calm Belt">Calm Belt</a> to reach <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a>, where Luffy had been recuperating from his injuries and from the loss of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a>. From there, he helped Luffy break into Marineford with <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> in order for him to send the secret message to his crew. Rayleigh also mentored Luffy on how to master all three different forms of <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> over the course of a year and a half. Luffy strongly respected Rayleigh as a teacher as he was even willing to endure hunger as punishment.<sup id="cite_ref-c894_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c894-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the two-year timeskip, it is apparent that both of them became close from their training together. As he headed towards <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Luffy shouted to Rayleigh that he would become the Pirate King, leaving Rayleigh with a smile and tears in his eyes. Rayleigh himself later proudly proclaimed Luffy as his pupil to the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>. When Luffy set sail, Rayleigh compared his late captain to Luffy, claiming that destiny is slowly but surely taking shape, and that Luffy has become a man well fit to wear that <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat#Gol_D._Roger/Shanks/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Straw Hat">Straw Hat</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh also seems to have developed a friendship with the former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>. At first, Jinbe could not believe his eyes when he saw Rayleigh in Amazon Lily. He took part in stealing a Marine ship, circling around Marineford, and the ringing of the Ox Bell.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Boa_Hancock">Boa Hancock</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Due to her hellish experience at the hands of the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Hancock</a> has a bitter hatred towards all men. However, Rayleigh is one of the few exceptions to this hatred since he helped Hancock and her sisters return to Amazon Lily after they escaped from <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>. While her sisters were shocked to see Silvers Rayleigh on Amazon Lily, Hancock remained single-minded about Luffy, only realizing later that Rayleigh was there. Hancock also permitted him to stay in Amazon Lily. Later, after parting ways with Jinbe, Hancock took Luffy and Rayleigh to <a href="/wiki/Rusukaina_Island" class="mw-redirect" title="Rusukaina Island">Rusukaina Island</a> for Luffy's special training. She said she would bring food for Luffy every day from Amazon Lily. When Rayleigh told her that no women would be allowed on the island during Luffy's training, she was furious but calmed down when Rayleigh told her that it was all for Luffy's own good. After the abolition of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>, both he and <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> would go to <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a> to help out the <a href="/wiki/Kuja" title="Kuja">Kuja</a> where he would run into <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, attacking the island and making a deal with him and the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, for Hancock to reverse her <a href="/wiki/Mero_Mero_no_Mi" title="Mero Mero no Mi">devil fruit</a> effect and then everyone leave afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059p15_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059p15-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gloriosa">Gloriosa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Gloriosa" title="Gloriosa">Gloriosa</a> is good friends with Rayleigh and Shakky. In the past, specifically during the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a> they were enemies on opposing crews, however they eventually became close friends as Rayleigh is one of the few (if not only) people who refer to her by her birth name, Gloriosa. Before her return to Amazon Lily, Gloriosa lived with Rayleigh and <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakky</a> on Sabaody Archipelago while sheltering the <a href="/wiki/Gorgon_Sisters" title="Gorgon Sisters">Gorgon Sisters</a> after their escape from the World Nobles.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh is an enemy of the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. He is one of the few people who know the true history and was willing to tell Robin about the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>, but she denied wanting to know further. The Government considers such people a great threat.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the past, Rayleigh and the other Roger Pirates encountered several <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, especially <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a>. The fact that he was a member of one of the strongest pirate crew made him a formidable enemy of the Marines. When Rayleigh fought Kizaru, he told him that if he were to get rid of his wanted poster, he could go into peaceful retirement. This means that Rayleigh still has an active bounty, though the amount has yet to be revealed. Kizaru replied that Rayleigh's bounty cannot simply be forgotten, as being a pirate, especially a Roger Pirate, carries the crimes throughout one's entire life.<sup id="cite_ref-Bounty_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bounty-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whitebeard_Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As a member of the Roger Pirates, Rayleigh had a rivalry with the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>. Nevertheless, as with his captain, Rayleigh has great respect for <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a> and even shed a tear for the man's death at the pinnacle of the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Chinjao">Chinjao</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Chinjao" title="Chinjao">Chinjao</a> apparently holds a grudge against Rayleigh, as when Luffy reveals Rayleigh is the one who taught him to control Haki, Chinjao expressed displeasure to know the Pirate King's right hand still lives.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Blackbeard">Blackbeard</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Even when Rayleigh first met <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a> years ago back when he was still a member of the Whitebeard Pirates, while both the Roger and Whitebeard Pirates were rivals, despite Rayleigh having some respect for Whitebeard's crew, Teach was the only member on that crew to whom Rayleigh despised. This hatred would grow, for not only in Blackbeard's actions in killing his former captain, but also for stealing Whitebeard's powers and claiming his territories for his own. Rayleigh continued to despise Blackbeard even more after the latter invaded <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a> and tried to kill Boa Hancock. While Rayleigh was successful in scaring off the Emperor and foiling his plan, Rayleigh admitted he would not win if he fought Blackbeard head on.
</p><p>Due to Teach's original role as an apprentice pirate on the Whitebeard Pirates, Rayleigh mockingly called him "Whitebeard's Cabin Boy" when he confronted the latter at Amazon Lily.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_2">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Although the two have never met each other, Rayleigh considers Vegapunk a fool for revealing many secrets about the Void Century to the world, which he considers something that people of their age should not talk about as it is something that people of the younger generations should figure out for themselves.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Awesome... the Pirate King's crew can defeat a monster like that without touching it.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Luffy after witnessing Rayleigh's Haki</cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
As the former "Right Hand of the Pirate King", Rayleigh is an extremely skilled and powerful combatant. Despite his old age, <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> stated that he was "100 times stronger" than all of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Eleven Supernovas</a> by the time they first arrived on the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> In his younger days with Gol D. Roger, Rayleigh participated in many battles against the  <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>,  <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>, making him a true veteran and one of the most experienced pirates in the world. He also commanded the rest of Roger's crew as his first mate and held several duties, like supervising his subordinates, including the young apprentices <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> was informed that Rayleigh may be on the Sabaody Archipelago, he told his men not to confront him, nor should <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> be informed. Garp reasoned that the Marines should not confront two legends, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> and Rayleigh, at the same time and even admitted that if the Marines were to make an honest attempt at capturing Rayleigh, they would need to do serious preparation if they did not want to lose countless soldiers in the attempt, a true testament to his extraordinary strength.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> His reputation alone was enough to have <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> who had spent two years mastering the <a href="/wiki/Yami_Yami_no_Mi" title="Yami Yami no Mi">Yami Yami no Mi</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a>, to retreat from <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059p16_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059p16-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh's immense battle prowess allowed him to fight on par with <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>, preventing him from attacking the Straw Hat Pirates. However, he himself has admitted that he is not as young as he used to be, and as a result can tire in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He also stated that due to his old age, he would likely be incapable of defeating Blackbeard.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059p16_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059p16-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> This implies that when he was in the prime of his strength, he might have been able to beat both Admiral Kizaru and pose a serious threat to Blackbeard. <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a> himself even states that Rayleigh was a "legend".<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh is also an expert in the coating business, as he performs such operations for various pirate ships heading down to <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> and he understands the workings of deep-sea currents.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Intelligence">Intelligence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Rayleigh has an extremely crafty and cunning mentality; he has managed to evade the grasp of the expansive World Government for over 20 years and quickly learned to exploit the slave-trading business on Sabaody Archipelago for personal gain (getting himself caught and sold to a wealthy bidder, before escaping and robbing his "master"). Calm and level-headed at virtually any and all times, he was the individual to break up arguments and disputes aboard the Oro Jackson, as first mate and the right-hand man to Gol D. Roger himself.
</p><p>Rayleigh knows the "true history" of the world from his time with Roger. However, he has also stated that, as a pirate crew lacking the archaeological knowledge of scholars of <a href="/wiki/Ohara" title="Ohara">Ohara</a>'s caliber, they could have interpreted that information differently than the Ohara scholars.<sup id="cite_ref-c507_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c507-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> However, this is questionable given the Roger Pirates had Kouzuki Oden, who possessed the knowledge on how to read and write the language on the Poneglyphs.
</p><p>Another noticeable trait of Rayleigh is his incredible perceptive and deduction capability. This is shown when he was (within a matter of moments) easily able to deduce what had happened after ending up on the slave auction stage on the Sabaody Archipelago.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Rayleigh possesses immense physical strength despite his elderly age. He was capable of killing several <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a> with his bare hands even after swimming to Amazon Lily from outside the Calm Belt.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, he could throw bullets with extreme force and accuracy to destroy cannonballs fired at him.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh is extremely fast and possesses extraordinary reflexes. When removing Camie's exploding collar, he patiently calculated the time when the collar released itself and quickly tossed it away before it detonated.<sup id="cite_ref-c504_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c504-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He could also intercept Kizaru's attack when the admiral was about to kill <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and also managed to keep up with his <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">light-enhanced</a> speed.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Rayleigh is a tremendously skilled and powerful swordsman with decades of combat experience since his time with the Roger Pirates. He was able to fight on equal grounds with Admiral Kizaru, who himself is a highly skilled swordsman when wielding his <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Ama no Murakumo</a>, and managed to cut and draw blood from the admiral's face by combining Armament Haki with his swordsmanship. This is even more impressive given that Rayleigh has not used his sword in quite a while due to being retired.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He can also create powerful compressed air slashes, as shown when he cut the ground to prevent Marines from chasing after Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Rayleigh is one of the very few people in the world who can use all three types of Haki. He is also a capable teacher, as he taught Luffy about each type of Haki and trained him in the basics.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120815061647" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Using Supreme King Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Using Supreme King Haki.gif" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120815061647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120815061647" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Using Supreme King Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120815061647" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Using Supreme King Haki.gif" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120815061647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Using_Supreme_King_Haki.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh using Supreme King Haki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rayleigh possesses immense mastery in the usage of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, a rare form of Haki that only one in several million people in the world can use. His level of skill is enough to render a specific target or entire crowds completely unconscious, as shown when he knocked out <a href="/wiki/Shalria" title="Shalria">Shalria</a> before disabling an entire hall room of hostiles.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Rayleigh's Supreme King Haki was at least twice as potent as Luffy's by the time of the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island_Arc" title="Fish-Man Island Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</a>; Rayleigh could have knocked out all 100,000 of the <a href="/wiki/New_Fish-Man_Pirates" title="New Fish-Man Pirates">New Fish-Man Pirates</a> opposing the Straw Hats, whereas Luffy overwhelmed only half that.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Most notably, he is among the small "handful" of users who are capable of using the advanced application of this type of Haki, able to "infuse" his body or objects with Supreme King Haki to increase his attack power, signified by thin streams of black lightning emanating from his body.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059p15_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059p15-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, he visibly infuses his sword with this Haki along with his body with notable lightning that incapacitates several Blackbeard Pirates in the area.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh is a master of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, which allowed him to kick and redirect an attack from Kizaru,<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> and hurt Luffy with a simple flick.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He is able to imbue his Haki into certain parts of his body or objects to harden them<sup id="cite_ref-c894_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c894-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and emit his Haki, an advanced application, to repel and injure opponents without touching them directly.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He is also able to use a high-grade version of this technique, in which he channels his Haki into his opponent or objects and destroys his opponent or objects from the inside out.<sup id="cite_ref-c504_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c504-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, when Rayleigh uses advanced Armament Haki, it is shown as a red-colored flowing aura. In the anime, he was able to block a kick from <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">hybrid form</a> with a single Armament coated finger.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh is a master of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>. He could sense that there were five hundred creatures on <a href="/wiki/Rusukaina" title="Rusukaina">Rusukaina</a> who were stronger than Luffy before his training had begun and used it to dodge an elephant's attack with his eyes closed.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> When he arrived at Amazon Lily, Rayleigh was able to sense that Luffy was on the island.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> He also has knowledge of the advanced application of this type of Haki and how high-level users can see into the future.<sup id="cite_ref-FutureHaki_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FutureHaki-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png/revision/latest?cb=20230210031326" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh&#39;s Sword" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh&#39;s Sword.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230210031326" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png/revision/latest?cb=20230210031326" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh&#39;s Sword" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230210031326" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh&#39;s Sword.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230210031326" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh%27s_Sword.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh's first sword.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rayleigh possesses a double-edged straight sword, with a cross hilt and a large round pommel, roughly half as long as his body height. When he defended Luffy from the Marines, he used a katana, which he keeps in a sheath.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
