<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913095101" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh and Roger Meet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh and Roger Meet.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095101" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913095101" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh and Roger Meet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095101" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh and Roger Meet.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095101" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_and_Roger_Meet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh and Roger's first meeting.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During his youth, Rayleigh stole a ship due to his house burning down and needing a place to live. Sometime after that, he met <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, who was impressed by the ship. Roger said that it was a fated meeting and asked Rayleigh to join him. Rayleigh simply laughed at his invitation and declined his offer.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Despite his initial refusal, Rayleigh later engaged in piracy and became first mate of the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>.
</p><p>38 years ago, Rayleigh and the Roger Pirates accompanied Roger on the island of <a href="/wiki/God_Valley" title="God Valley">God Valley</a> to do battle with <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/God%27s_Knights" title="God&#39;s Knights">God's Knights</a>, taking part in what would later be known as the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> After leaving God Valley the Roger pirates were partying over the treasures which they stole when they discovered a <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">baby</a> inside one of the treasure chests.<sup id="cite_ref-4billion_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4billion-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>28 years before the current storyline, Roger fell ill from an incurable disease, leading the crew to take one final journey together and ventured into the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> together. At some point Rayleigh scolded <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> for constantly arguing over whether the North pole or South pole was colder, and shortly after joined the rest of the crew in a battle against an unnamed enemy ship.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> at <a href="/wiki/Edd_War" title="Edd War">Edd War</a>, Buggy panicked at the potential conflict between two infamous pirate crews: the Roger Pirates and the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Lion_Pirates" title="Golden Lion Pirates">Golden Lion Pirates</a>. Rayleigh was present, and he held <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> back, telling him not to worry. When Roger rejected <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>'s offer to become his right-hand man, Rayleigh prepared for battle along with the other Roger Pirates. A battle between the two crews ensued, and a change in the weather allowed the Roger Pirates to sink half of Shiki's ships.<sup id="cite_ref-ch0_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch0-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point 26 years ago, the Roger Pirates were causing a ruckus on an island. After defeating a group of <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, they learned that the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> docked on the other side of the island.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> The Roger Pirates were then confronted by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>. Rayleigh and <a href="/wiki/Scopper_Gaban" title="Scopper Gaban">Scopper Gaban</a> prepared to fight him, but Roger charged in and blew Oden away with a single slash. The Roger Pirates clashed with the Whitebeard Pirates for three days. After the battle, the crews formed a truce and exchanged gifts. The Roger Pirates were later joined by Oden and his family as well as <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>. At some point, the Roger Pirates visited <a href="/wiki/Skypiea" title="Skypiea">Skypiea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png/revision/latest?cb=20210404035607" class="image"><img alt="Roger Pirates Laughing" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Roger Pirates Laughing.png" data-image-key="Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210404035607" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png/revision/latest?cb=20210404035607" class="image"><img alt="Roger Pirates Laughing" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210404035607" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Roger Pirates Laughing.png" data-image-key="Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210404035607" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Roger_Pirates_Laughing.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh and the Roger Pirates celebrating reaching Laugh Tale.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After leaving Skypiea, the crew's voyage took them to <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tequila_Wolf" title="Tequila Wolf">Tequila Wolf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a>. Sometime later, they left <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Kouzuki Toki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Momonosuke</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Hiyori</a>, Inuarashi, and Nekomamushi at <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. Sometime after the visit to <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>, the Roger Pirates finally reached <a href="/wiki/Laugh_Tale" title="Laugh Tale">Laugh Tale</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A year before his death, Roger disbanded the crew in secret. Roger was the first to leave and the crew tearfully parted ways with him. They later returned Oden to Wano Country, and they bid farewell to him as well.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before he handed himself over to the Marines, Roger told Rayleigh that he would not die. Unwilling to watch the execution of his closest friend, Rayleigh toasted a drink to the man with a laugh as the blades passed and downed a glass as his first act in the Great Age of Piracy, the Age of Dreams.<sup id="cite_ref-c506_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c506-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Rayleigh stated that he laughed (and cried and drank) nonetheless upon hearing the message Roger had left the world.
</p><p>Sometime later, Rayleigh was saved by a young <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a> from drowning in a shipwreck. Since then, Rayleigh has been on good terms with Hachi. He, along with <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gloriosa" title="Gloriosa">Nyon</a>, also helped protect the <a href="/wiki/Gorgon_Sisters" title="Gorgon Sisters">Gorgon Sisters</a> after their escape from <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slavery</a> from the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>. Eventually, Rayleigh became a coating mechanic on <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a> and at some point, married Shakuyaku.<sup id="cite_ref-marriage_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marriage-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When news of Shiki's escape reached Rayleigh, he remarked on it and wondered what Shiki was up to.<sup id="cite_ref-ch0_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch0-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>12 years prior to the series, Rayleigh met his former apprentice <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> again and noticed the latter lost his arm and his hat. Rayleigh asked him what occurred as he told him of a <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">boy</a> that he met in the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a> who had the same passion as his former captain. Intrigued, Rayleigh desired to meet this boy someday.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He had been missing for six months prior to Luffy's arrival on the archipelago.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Episode_A">One Piece Episode A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a> came across Rayleigh when they needed to have their ship coated in order to reach Fish-Man Island, with the <a href="/wiki/Masked_Deuce" title="Masked Deuce">Masked Deuce</a> and him hitting it off. Rayleigh then coated their ship, with none of the Spade Pirates, except for <a href="/wiki/Skull" title="Skull">Skull</a> realizing who he was.
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh let himself be captured to be sold as a slave, and when the <a href="/wiki/Merfolk" title="Merfolk">mermaid</a> <a href="/wiki/Camie" title="Camie">Camie</a> was brought into the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a>, Rayleigh discreetly used <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> to knock out <a href="/wiki/Disco" title="Disco">Disco</a>, although his fellow slave <a href="/wiki/Stansen" title="Stansen">Stansen</a> recognized what he did.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> As an auction took place, Rayleigh broke out of his cell and stole the money that people had bid for their slaves before making his way to the auction stage. There, he saw <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a> and ascertained that he and his allies, the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, had attacked a <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a> to save Camie. Rayleigh then unleashed Supreme King Haki, knocking out most of the people in the auction hall, and he recognized <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, saying he had wanted to meet the Straw Hat captain.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913095312" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Helping Hatchi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Helping Hatchi.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095312" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913095312" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Helping Hatchi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095312" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Helping Hatchi.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913095312" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Helping_Hatchi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh thanking Luffy for protecting Hatchan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rayleigh then grabbed Camie's exploding collar and ripped it off, tossing it aside before it could explode. He surveyed the room and saw that the <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a>, along with the Straw Hats, had survived his Haki blast, and he then turned his attention to Hatchan, thanking the Straw Hats for protecting him. The pirates then headed out of the auction hall, and Rayleigh told the Straw Hats to meet him at Grove 13 later.<sup id="cite_ref-c504_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c504-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> After the three pirate crews had fought through the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> laying siege to the auction house, Rayleigh was able to run off with Hatchan.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/RayleighVoidCentury.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913100713" class="image"><img alt="RayleighVoidCentury" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="RayleighVoidCentury.png" data-image-key="RayleighVoidCentury.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/RayleighVoidCentury.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913100713" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/RayleighVoidCentury.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913100713" class="image"><img alt="RayleighVoidCentury" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/RayleighVoidCentury.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913100713" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="RayleighVoidCentury.png" data-image-key="RayleighVoidCentury.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/RayleighVoidCentury.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913100713" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:RayleighVoidCentury.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Robin asks Rayleigh about the Void Century.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rayleigh and the Straw Hats made it to <a href="/wiki/Shakky%27s_Rip-off_Bar" title="Shakky&#39;s Rip-off Bar">Shakky's Rip-off Bar</a> with Hatchan, Camie, and <a href="/wiki/Pappag" title="Pappag">Pappag</a>, and Rayleigh revealed to Luffy who he was and how he knew Hatchan. He then revealed to the Straw Hats what had really happened to Roger, and they talked about <a href="/wiki/Crocus" title="Crocus">Crocus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> then asked Rayleigh about the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a> and Roger's writing on the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyph</a> in <a href="/wiki/Skypiea" title="Skypiea">Skypiea</a> but opted to continue researching for herself after Rayleigh warned about how she might use the information. <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> then asked if the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> existed, but was stopped by Luffy, who wanted to discover the One Piece for himself. Rayleigh asked Luffy if he really intended to conquer the New World, as Luffy states he will become the freest man on the sea if he is Pirate King. Rayleigh was impressed by his ideology, seeing the similarities to Roger like Shanks saw. Rayleigh then went to coat the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Straw Hats' ship</a>, not charging them anything in return for them helping Hatchan, and gave them his <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a>, telling them to find him in three days.<sup id="cite_ref-c507_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c507-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/41/Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20230821015847" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Stopping Kizaru" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Stopping Kizaru.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/41/Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230821015847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/41/Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png/revision/latest?cb=20230821015847" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Stopping Kizaru" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/41/Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230821015847" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Stopping Kizaru.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/41/Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230821015847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Stopping_Kizaru.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh redirecting Kizaru's attack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A short time later, Marine Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> came and attacked the Straw Hats, but before he could kill <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, Rayleigh came in and intercepted him.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Rayleigh tried to see if Kizaru would leave the Straw Hats alone, but Kizaru would not abandon his mission. The Straw Hats immediately started running away, and Kizaru attempted to go after them, but Rayleigh stopped him with a sword.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> As Rayleigh sparred with Kizaru, he witnessed <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> joining some <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifistas</a> who were attacking the Straw Hats and saw as Kuma made the Straw Hats disappear. Kuma then went to Rayleigh and revealed that he was an officer of the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> and was acting to help the Straw Hats escape.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Rayleigh watched as Kuma then transported the remaining Straw Hats off the island.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101003" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Cries for Whitebeard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Cries for Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101003" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101003" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Cries for Whitebeard" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101003" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Cries for Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101003" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Cries_for_Whitebeard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh shedding a tear for Whitebeard's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Whitebeard's death was aired at Sabaody, Rayleigh, who had escaped Kizaru's arrest, watched from afar while drinking. He remarked that Whitebeard was finally dead with a smile on his face and tears in his eyes.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, Rayleigh set off on a ship to <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a>. However, before he could even reach the <a href="/wiki/Calm_Belt" title="Calm Belt">Calm Belt</a>, his ship sank in a storm and thus forced him to swim the rest of the way to the island. He killed several <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a> when he was getting closer to the shore of the island, something which surprised and almost frightened the Heart Pirates who were watching from the shore. When he got to the shore, he remembered <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> from the Sabaody Archipelago and told them he thought Luffy was on the island.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101623" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Meets With Sandersonia, Marigold and Gloriosa" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Meets With Sandersonia, Marigold and Gloriosa.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101623" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Meets With Sandersonia, Marigold and Gloriosa" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101623" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Meets With Sandersonia, Marigold and Gloriosa.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia%2C_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Meets_With_Sandersonia,_Marigold_and_Gloriosa.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh reunites with Sandersonia, Marigold, and Nyon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He saw Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> coming toward him. When Luffy asked about his crew, Rayleigh said he doubted they were all back yet. After telling Luffy that Law said to take it easy for another two weeks, he proceeded to greet Nyon, Boa Hancock, and her sisters, whom he had met 13 years ago; he had protected them when they had escaped from the Celestial Dragons. Elder Nyon is an old friend of his, and Rayleigh passed on a message from Shakky. He reassured them that the Marines would not even think to look for Luffy on Amazon Lily and that he was completely safe there.
</p><p>Rayleigh recalled what Kuma whispered to him back on the archipelago. He explained that Kuma told him about the general direction in which he sent Luffy, which happened to lead right to Amazon Lily. After going back through the events of the war with Shakky, she was able to surmise (correctly on all three accounts) that Boa Hancock was hiding Luffy on her home island, that she was doing so out of love for Luffy, and also as a means of hiding him from the Marines. Rayleigh commented that a woman's intuition was a truly frightening thing. He said he would get to the main reason he came to find Luffy. Rayleigh asked him if he wanted to return to Sabaody, and Luffy replied yes. Rayleigh reminded him of what happened there before, saying that gathering his crew there again would lead to the same result as before. He started to propose an idea he has to Luffy, giving him the choice of rejecting it if he so chooses.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He infiltrated Marineford with Luffy and Jinbe and took part in stealing a Marine ship and circling Marineford once with it. He was on the <a href="/wiki/Perfume_Yuda" title="Perfume Yuda">Perfume Yuda</a>, with two <a href="/wiki/Kuja_Pirates" title="Kuja Pirates">Kuja Pirates</a> pulling on his cheek. He told Luffy that his crew most likely got the meaning of his message, due to its abnormal nature, and said that he had a hunch that the others would understand the message.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230624012410" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh&#39;s Armament Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh&#39;s Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624012410" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230624012410" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh&#39;s Armament Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624012410" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh&#39;s Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a1/Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624012410" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh%27s_Armament_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh demonstrating Armament Haki to Luffy on an attacking elephant.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He and Luffy went to <a href="/wiki/Rusukaina" title="Rusukaina">Rusukaina</a> for special training. Rayleigh told Hancock that none of the Kujas are allowed on the island during the training and that if she was worried, then she should pray for Luffy. Once the Kuja Pirates left, Rayleigh began Luffy's training by mentioning that the island was once inhabited, but the chaotic climate changes and the ferocious nature of the wildlife eventually killed all the natives. As a wild elephant came charging at them, Rayleigh explained the basic concepts of Haki, using the elephant as a demonstration for them. Rayleigh told Luffy that there are three kinds of Haki: Observation Haki, Armament Haki, and Supreme King Haki. He used Observation Haki to dodge the elephant's attack and used Armament Haki to repel the elephant. When Luffy started to understand Haki, Rayleigh subdued the elephant using the Supreme King Haki.
</p><p>The two began training on the island. Luffy realized that he had seen these techniques before in some form or another during his adventures. Rayleigh hoped to use those two years to teach him the basics of controlling the different types of Haki, as it would take longer with a normal person.<sup id="cite_ref-c597_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c597-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During Luffy's training, he developed <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a>. Luffy asked Rayleigh on how to improve its attack power, and Rayleigh warned him about the consequences of using this technique.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220811094242" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Training Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rayleigh Training Luffy.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220811094242" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220811094242" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Training Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220811094242" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rayleigh Training Luffy.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220811094242" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rayleigh_Training_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh training Luffy in Haki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While teaching Observation Haki to Luffy, he challenged Luffy to dodge 100 times while blindfolded or he would not be allowed to eat. When Luffy was attacking blindly, he accidentally hit Rayleigh's dinner, causing him to hit Luffy out of anger and annoyance as Luffy sensed his emotions. During a later conversation, Rayleigh remarked on how Luffy was proficient in sensing the feelings of living things. He also mentioned that there are people who can see a glimpse into the future with Observation Haki and asked Luffy what would he do if he met one of these people.<sup id="cite_ref-FutureHaki_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FutureHaki-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After teaching Luffy the basics of Haki, Rayleigh informed him that Haki can grow stronger when facing stronger foes.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Saga">Fish-Man Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Sabaody_Arc">Return to Sabaody Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101935" class="image"><img alt="Silvers Rayleigh&#39;s Return to Sabaody Archipelago" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Silvers Rayleigh&#39;s Return to Sabaody Archipelago.png" data-image-key="Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101935" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913101935" class="image"><img alt="Silvers Rayleigh&#39;s Return to Sabaody Archipelago" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101935" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Silvers Rayleigh&#39;s Return to Sabaody Archipelago.png" data-image-key="Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913101935" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Silvers_Rayleigh%27s_Return_to_Sabaody_Archipelago.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Rayleigh at Shakky's bar two years later.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rayleigh returned to Sabaody Archipelago half a year before Luffy. In Shakky's bar, he commented on how strong the Straw Hat Pirates had become. He also finished <a href="/wiki/Coating" title="Coating">coating</a> the Thousand Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rayleigh met Nami, Robin, Franky, Chopper, and Usopp on the Thousand Sunny. He informed them that Luffy had arrived on the island and is about to teach Nami on how to operate a coated ship. He told her to move the ship to Grove 42 and to wait until everyone assembled, saying it was finally time to restart.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Rayleigh went to Grove 46 to check up on Luffy. He also commented on how Luffy strengthened his Haki.
</p><p>After Luffy had declared that he would be the Pirate King, Rayleigh smiled with tears in his eyes.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> As the Marines begin their pursuit, Rayleigh drew a line on the ground with his sword and warned the Marines not to cross it, declaring that Luffy is his student. By doing so, he bought some extra time for the Straw Hat Pirates to escape to Fish-Man Island.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Once the Straw Hats left, he revealed in a conversation with Shakky that a previous owner of Luffy's straw hat was in fact, Roger. After reminiscing about the day, he first met Roger, Rayleigh started tearing up and commented that Luffy is a man worthy of that hat. Rayleigh added that it is not a bad idea to live a little longer.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500.2C000.2C000_Man_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500,000,000_Man_Arc">From the Decks of the World: The 500,000,000 Man Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Rayleigh was gambling while reading the news of the Straw Hats' new bounties after the events at Dressrosa.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the World Government abolished the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>, Rayleigh and Shakuyaku sailed to <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a>, which was already under attack by the Marines and the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>. Rayleigh threatened <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Teach</a> who was choking Hancock and intimidated him into letting her go.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059p15_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059p15-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Weeks after the attack on <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a> was over, Rayleigh sat with the current and former leaders of the island and discussed the situation and the Marines' new weapons, the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime later, during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>, Rayleigh got drunk at Shakky's bar while listening to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s world-wide message about the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>. When Vegapunk declared that the Roger Pirates had already discovered the full truth decades earlier, Rayleigh chastised Vegapunk for not letting the younger generation figure it out themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> As the broadcast neared its end, Rayleigh passed out drunk, with Shakky covering him with a blanket.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> vs. <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> (unseen)</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 152px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 152px; height: 152px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Silvers_Rayleigh_Young.png/revision/latest?cb=20130504091426" class="image"><img alt="Silvers Rayleigh Young" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="130" height="127" data-image-name="Silvers Rayleigh Young.png" data-image-key="Silvers_Rayleigh_Young.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Silvers_Rayleigh_Young.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20130504091426" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Rayleigh from Buggy's flashback as he appears in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 152px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 152px; height: 152px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Rayleigh_Buggy_Flashback_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20211211181404" class="image"><img alt="Rayleigh Buggy Flashback Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="93" height="130" data-image-name="Rayleigh Buggy Flashback Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Rayleigh_Buggy_Flashback_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Rayleigh_Buggy_Flashback_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/93?cb=20211211181404" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Rayleigh from Buggy's flashback in the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 152px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 152px; height: 152px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Young_Rayleigh_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215095530" class="image"><img alt="Young Rayleigh in the Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="130" height="95" data-image-name="Young Rayleigh in the Anime.png" data-image-key="Young_Rayleigh_in_the_Anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Young_Rayleigh_in_the_Anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/130?cb=20130215095530" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Rayleigh from Buggy's flashback as he appears in the anime.
</div></span></div>
<p>In the manga, when a younger Rayleigh's glasses were briefly seen, they had a circular shape. In the anime initially, they had an oblong shape. In the same flashback in the anime, his scar is missing, presumably because the scar is difficult to see in the manga.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Also, Rayleigh's hair was black instead of the strawberry blond seen in later flashbacks. This changing of a character's design to a more generic one occurs several times in the series, notably with <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>.
</p><p>Rayleigh mentioning his second suggestion to Luffy was not in the manga. In the manga, Rayleigh is the only one who fights the elephant. It was never shown in the manga how Luffy, Jinbe and Rayleigh got back into Marineford. In the anime, Luffy's actions in Marineford are seen, though in the manga they were only explained later.
</p><p>In the final battle between the Roger Pirates and the Whitebeard Pirates, Rayleigh was shown briefly clashing with Marco, using his advanced Armament to stop the latter's <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">attack</a> with a single finger. In the manga, the battle as a whole was little elaborated upon.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D62&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Rayleigh's name is similar to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Long_John_Silver" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Long John Silver">John Silver</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Treasure_Island" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Treasure Island">Treasure Island</a></i> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Raleigh" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Walter Raleigh">Sir Walter Raleigh</a>, an English 16th-century explorer and privateer. It should be noted that Sir Walter Raleigh's name has been spelled in over forty different ways, in which also includes the spelling "Rayleigh" (<i>note: the "y" would actually be pronounced as "i"</i>).</li>
<li>It is possible that his name is related to the phenomenon known as "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rayleigh_scattering" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rayleigh scattering">Rayleigh scattering</a>". In particular, when fighting <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>, Rayleigh was shown to be able to 'scatter' Kizaru's light attacks, which is a visual pun on Rayleigh Scattering, which involves the scattering of light.</li>
<li>When Rayleigh fought Kizaru, he told him that if he were to get rid of his wanted poster, he could go into a peaceful retirement. This means that Rayleigh has an active <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a>; the amount has yet to be revealed.<sup id="cite_ref-Bounty_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bounty-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Silver is traditionally considered the next most valuable metal after gold, and as the first mate, Silvers Rayleigh was the second highest ranked man in the crew after the captain, Gol D. Roger also known as Gold Roger.
<ul><li>There is a theme of rare metals among the senior members of the Roger Pirates, as another member is named <a href="/wiki/Scopper_Gaban" title="Scopper Gaban">Scopper Gaban</a>, as in "copper".</li></ul></li>
<li>Rayleigh is the first former pirate known to still have an active bounty.<sup id="cite_ref-Bounty_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bounty-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the 6th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan poll</a>, Rayleigh was ranked 38th.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Blue_Deep:_Characters_World" title="One Piece Blue Deep: Characters World">Blue Deep databook</a>, his relationship with Shakuyaku is written as that of friends, rather than husband and wife. As he was referred to as her "Uchi no hito" (うちの人; lit. person of my household) in the manga,<sup id="cite_ref-marriage_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marriage-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> their relationship as stated in the databook may be an oversight by Oda.</li>
<li>Rayleigh's favorite food is boiled beans.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Rayleigh is the first person to teach Luffy about Haki.</li>
<li>Rayleigh's epithet, <i>Meiō</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">冥王</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, lit. "dark king")</span>, is the Japanese word for Pluto/Hades, the god of the underworld in ancient Greco-Roman mythology.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSilvers_Rayleigh%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Rayleigh's birthday, May 13, comes from his epithet since 5-13 can be derived from Mei-Oo.<sup id="cite_ref-Birth_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Birth-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> were first revealed to be part of Roger's crew, a fan asked Oda in a <a href="/wiki/SBS" title="SBS">SBS question</a> if the man that scolded them was a subordinate captain under Roger that commanded the ship they were sailing on, or even a high-ranking officer. Without giving away Rayleigh's name at the time, Oda responded that this man was none other than the first mate of Roger's crew. Oda also stated in his response that since he had set this fact in stone from the very start, he told <a href="/wiki/Toei_Animation" title="Toei Animation">Toei Animation</a> that when they adapt Buggy's flashback for the anime, Buggy and Shanks should not refer to Rayleigh as <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> in the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
